This state will only be entered if\n    /// the [`SyncService`] has been built with the\n    /// [`SyncServiceBuilder::with_offline_mode`] setting.\n    ///\n    /// The [`SyncService`] will enter the offline mode if syncing with the\n    /// server fails, it will then periodically check if the server is\n    /// available using the `/_matrix/client/versions` endpoint.\n    ///\n    /// Once the [`SyncService`] receives a 200 response from the\n    /// `/_matrix/client/versions` endpoint, it will go back into the\n    /// [`State::Running`] mode and attempt to sync again.\n    ///\n    /// Calling [`SyncService::start()`] while in this state will abort the\n    /// `/_matrix/client/versions` checks and attempt to sync immediately.\n    ///\n    /// Calling [`SyncService::stop()`] will Here is the code-level cheat-sheet for matrix-rust-sdk 0.14, verified against the vendored sources.\n\n---\n\n# matrix-rust-sdk 0.14 API Cheat-Sheet\n\nAll signatures below were read from the unpacked crates in\n`~/.cargo/registry/src/index.crates.io-*/` — specifically `matrix-sdk-0.14.0`, `matrix-sdk-base-0.14.1`, `matrix-sdk-ui-0.14.0`, `matrix-sdk-sqlite-0.14.0`, `ruma-events-0.31.0`, `eyeball-im-0.7.0`.\n\n### Cargo features you must enable\n```toml\n[dependencies]\nmatrix-sdk = { version = \"0.14\", default-features = false, features = [\"sqlite\", \"e2e-encryption\"] }\n# \"rustls-tls\" or \"native-tls\" is also required (default features include one)\nmatrix-sdk-ui = \"0.14\"\ntokio = { version = \"1\", features = [\"full\"] }\n```\n- `sqlite` gates `ClientBuilder::sqlite_store` and the `Sqlite*` re-exports.\n- `e2e-encryption` turns on transparent encrypt/decrypt (see §8).\n\n### Consolidated `use` block (covers every snippet below)\n```rust\nuse matrix_sdk::{\n    Client, ClientBuildError,\n    // re-exported from matrix_sdk_base:\n    RoomState, RoomDisplayName, SessionMeta,\n    authentication::{matrix::MatrixSession, SessionTokens},\n    media::{MediaFormat, MediaRequestParameters, MediaThumbnailSettings},\n    store::RoomLoadSettings,\n    ruma::{\n        OwnedRoomId, RoomId, UserId, OwnedMxcUri,\n        api::client::media::get_content_thumbnail::v3::Method, // ruma::media::Method also works\n        events::room::{\n            MediaSource,\n            message::{RoomMessageEventContent, MessageType, AnyMessageLikeEventContent},\n        },\n    },\n};\nuse matrix_sdk_ui::{\n    Timeline,\n    sync_service::{SyncService, State as SyncState},\n    room_list_service::{\n        RoomListService, RoomList,\n        filters::new_filter_non_left,\n    },\n    timeline::{\n        RoomExt,                       // brings `room.timeline()` / `room.timeline_builder()`\n        TimelineItem, TimelineItemContent, EventTimelineItem,\n        VirtualTimelineItem,\n        MsgLikeKind, MsgLikeContent, Message,\n        RoomMembershipChange,\n    },\n};\nuse eyeball_im::{Vector, VectorDiff};\nuse futures_util::{StreamExt, pin_mut};\nuse std::sync::Arc;\n```\n\n---\n\n## 1. Build a Client\n\n`ClientBuilder` (`matrix-sdk-0.14.0/src/client/builder/mod.rs`). Homeserver/server-name setters are mutually exclusive.\n\n```rust\nlet client: Client = Client::builder()\n    .homeserver_url(\"https://matrix.example.org\")     // fn homeserver_url(impl AsRef<str>)\n    // or: .server_name(<&ServerName>)  /  .server_name_or_homeserver_url(\"example.org\")\n    .sqlite_store(\"/path/to/store_dir\", Some(\"db-passphrase\")) // #[cfg(sqlite)]\n    .build()                                            // async\n    .await?;                                            // -> Result<Client, ClientBuildError>\n```\n\n- `pub fn sqlite_store(self, path: impl AsRef<Path>, passphrase: Option<&str>) -> Self` — path is a **directory**, passphrase is `Option<&str>` (Some encrypts the SQLCipher DB; also encrypts the crypto store). Internally builds `SqliteStoreConfig::new(path).passphrase(passphrase)`.\n- Related: `.sqlite_store_with_cache_path(path, cache_path, passphrase)`, `.store_config(StoreConfig)`, `.with_encryption_settings(EncryptionSettings)`, `.cross_process_store_locks_holder_name(String)`.\n- `build()` returns `Result<Client, ClientBuildError>`. (`Client::new(url: Url)` also exists but has no persistence.)\n\n## 2. Login + Session persistence/restore\n\n`MatrixAuth` via `client.matrix_auth()` (`authentication/matrix/mod.rs`, `login_builder.rs`).\n\n```rust\nlet auth = client.matrix_auth();\n\n// LoginBuilder implements IntoFuture, so `.await` == `.send().await`.\nauth.login_username(\"@alice:example.org\", \"password\")   // -> LoginBuilder\n    .initial_device_display_name(\"My Rust Client\")\n    // .device_id(\"EXISTINGDEVICE\")                      // optional, to reuse a device\n    .await?;                                             // -> Result<login::v3::Response>\n\n// Grab the session to persist (serde Serialize/Deserialize):\nlet session: MatrixSession = auth.session().expect(\"logged in\"); // Option<MatrixSession>\nlet json = serde_json::to_string(&session)?;   // save json + the homeserver URL somewhere\n```\n\n`MatrixSession` (`matrix_sdk::authentication::matrix::MatrixSession`) is:\n```rust\npub struct MatrixSession {\n    pub meta:   SessionMeta,    // { user_id: OwnedUserId, device_id: OwnedDeviceId }  (matrix_sdk::SessionMeta)\n    pub tokens: SessionTokens,  // { access_token: String, refresh_token: Option<String> }\n}\n```\n\nRestore on next launch (build the Client the same way first, then):\n```rust\nlet session: MatrixSession = serde_json::from_str(&json)?;\n\n// Simplest — top-level Client method, single arg (uses RoomLoadSettings::All):\nclient.restore_session(session).await?;        // fn restore_session(impl Into<AuthSession>) -> Result<()>\n\n// Equivalent lower-level form REQUIRES a second RoomLoadSettings arg (differs from your note):\n// client.matrix_auth().restore_session(session, RoomLoadSettings::default()).await?;\n```\n⚠️ `MatrixAuth::restore_session` takes **two** args in 0.14: `(session, room_load_settings)`. The one-arg call you described is `Client::restore_session`. `RoomLoadSettings` is `matrix_sdk::store::RoomLoadSettings` (`::default()` == `All`).\n\n## 3. Sync (high-level, via matrix-sdk-ui)\n\n`SyncService` (`matrix-sdk-ui-0.14.0/src/sync_service.rs`) is the recommended driver — it owns and runs the `RoomListService` (sliding sync) + encryption sync in the background.\n\n```rust\nlet sync_service: SyncService = SyncService::builder(client.clone())\n    .build()          // async -> Result<SyncService, Error>\n    .await?;\n\nsync_service.start().await;                    // async, returns () — spawns background tasks\n\nlet room_list_service: Arc<RoomListService> = sync_service.room_list_service();\n\n// Observe state (eyeball::Subscriber<State> is a Stream):\nlet mut state = sync_service.state();          // -> Subscriber<matrix_sdk_ui::sync_service::State>\n// State variants: Idle | Running | Terminated | Error | Offline\n// ...\nsync_service.stop().await;                     // graceful shutdown\n```\nGet the `RoomListService` from the `SyncService` (don't construct it yourself). `RoomListService::new(client)` exists but then you must drive `.sync()` manually.\n\n## 4. Room list\n\n`RoomList` / dynamic entries (`room_list_service/room_list.rs`). The element type is `matrix_sdk::Room` (re-exported as `matrix_sdk_ui::room_list_service::Room`).\n\n```rust\nlet room_list: RoomList = room_list_service.all_rooms().await?;   // async -> Result<RoomList, Error>\n\n// page_size: usize. Returns a diff stream + a controller you MUST configure.\nlet (stream, controller) = room_list.entries_with_dynamic_adapters(200);\npin_mut!(stream);\n\n// ⚠️ Without a filter + a page, the list stays empty:\ncontroller.set_filter(Box::new(new_filter_non_left())); // BoxedFilterFn\ncontroller.add_one_page();                              // reveal page_size entries\n\n// Consume batched diffs. Item type: Vec<VectorDiff<Room>>\nwhile let Some(diffs) = stream.next().await {\n    for diff in diffs {\n        match diff {\n            VectorDiff::Reset { values }     => { /* Vector<Room> full reset */ }\n            VectorDiff::Append { values }     => { /* ... */ }\n            VectorDiff::PushBack { value }    => { /* Room */ }\n            VectorDiff::Insert { index, value } => {}\n            VectorDiff::Set { index, value }  => {}\n            VectorDiff::Remove { index }      => {}\n            VectorDiff::PushFront { value }   => {}\n            VectorDiff::PopFront | VectorDiff::PopBack | VectorDiff::Clear => {}\n            VectorDiff::Truncate { length }   => {}\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n`VectorDiff` full variant set (eyeball-im 0.7): `Append, Clear, PushFront, PushBack, PopFront, PopBack, Insert, Set, Remove, Truncate, Reset`.\n\nPer-`Room` accessors (mix of `matrix_sdk::Room` and its `Deref` target `matrix_sdk_base::Room`):\n```rust\nroom.room_id();                                   // -> &RoomId\nroom.display_name().await?;                       // async -> RoomDisplayName  (StoreResult)\nroom.cached_display_name();                        // -> Option<RoomDisplayName>  (sync, no I/O)\nroom.avatar_url();                                 // -> Option<OwnedMxcUri>\nroom.unread_notification_counts();                 // -> UnreadNotificationsCount { notification_count: u64, highlight_count: u64 }\nroom.num_unread_messages();                        // -> u64\nroom.num_unread_notifications();                   // -> u64\nroom.num_unread_mentions();                        // -> u64\nroom.state();                                      // -> RoomState (Joined | Left | Invited | Knocked | Banned)\n```\n`RoomDisplayName` enum: `Named(String) | Aliased(String) | Calculated(String) | EmptyWas(String) | Empty` (impl `Display`).\n\n**Latest-event preview:** there is no `Room::latest_event()`. Two options:\n- Build a `Timeline` (§5) and call `timeline.latest_event().await -> Option<EventTimelineItem>`.\n- Call `room_list_service.subscribe_to_rooms(&[room_id]).await` (sets up `LatestEventValue` via `client.latest_events()`), then read through the latest-events API. For a first pass, the Timeline approach is simplest.\n\n## 5. Timeline\n\nBring `RoomExt` into scope (`matrix_sdk_ui::timeline::RoomExt`), then:\n```rust\nlet timeline: Timeline = room.timeline().await?;   // == room.timeline_builder().build().await\n// or: room.timeline_builder().with_focus(TimelineFocus::Live { hide_threaded_events: false }).build().await?\n```\n\nInitial items + live diff stream:\n```rust\n// (Vector<Arc<TimelineItem>>, impl Stream<Item = Vec<VectorDiff<Arc<TimelineItem>>>>)\nlet (items, mut stream) = timeline.subscribe().await;\n// let items = timeline.items().await;             // Vector<Arc<TimelineItem>>, no stream\n\ntimeline.paginate_backwards(50).await?;            // async fn(num_events: u16) -> Result<bool>  (true == hit start)\ntimeline.paginate_forwards(50).await?;             // for non-live focuses\n```\n\nInspect an item (`timeline/item.rs`, `event_item/mod.rs`, `event_item/content/*`):\n```rust\nfor item in &items {\n    let item: &Arc<TimelineItem> = item;\n    if let Some(ev) = item.as_event() {            // Option<&EventTimelineItem>\n        let sender: &UserId = ev.sender();\n        let ts = ev.timestamp();                   // MilliSecondsSinceUnixEpoch (.0 = UInt ms)\n        let mine = ev.is_own();                    // bool\n        // ev.event_id() -> Option<&EventId>, ev.sender_profile() -> &TimelineDetails<Profile>\n\n        match ev.content() {                        // &TimelineItemContent\n            TimelineItemContent::MsgLike(MsgLikeContent { kind, .. }) => match kind {\n                MsgLikeKind::Message(msg) => {\n                    let body: &str = msg.body();           // plain-text body\n                    match msg.msgtype() {                  // &MessageType\n                        MessageType::Text(t)   => { /* t.body, t.formatted */ }\n                        MessageType::Image(i)  => { /* i.source: MediaSource, i.info */ }\n                        MessageType::Notice(n) => {}\n                        MessageType::Emote(e)  => {}\n                        MessageType::File(_) | MessageType::Audio(_) | MessageType::Video(_) => {}\n                        _ => {}\n                    }\n                }\n                MsgLikeKind::Sticker(_)          => {}\n                MsgLikeKind::Poll(_)             => {}\n                MsgLikeKind::Redacted            => {}\n                MsgLikeKind::UnableToDecrypt(_)  => {}   // encrypted, no keys yet\n            },\n            TimelineItemContent::MembershipChange(RoomMembershipChange { .. }) => {} // join/leave/ban/invite\n            TimelineItemContent::ProfileChange(_) => {}   // display-name / avatar change\n            TimelineItemContent::OtherState(_)    => {}   // other state events\n            TimelineItemContent::CallInvite | TimelineItemContent::CallNotify => {}\n            TimelineItemContent::FailedToParseMessageLike { .. }\n            | TimelineItemContent::FailedToParseState { .. } => {}\n        }\n    } else if let Some(v) = item.as_virtual() {     // Option<&VirtualTimelineItem>\n        match v { VirtualTimelineItem::DateDivider(ts) => {},\n                  VirtualTimelineItem::ReadMarker => {},\n                  VirtualTimelineItem::TimelineStart => {} }\n    }\n}\n```\n⚠️ **Big 0.14 shape change vs. your description:** `TimelineItemContent` is *not* flat. Text/image/notice/sticker/poll/redacted/UTD are all nested under `MsgLike(MsgLikeContent { kind: MsgLikeKind::* })`; only membership/profile/other-state/call/parse-failures are top-level variants. Convenience accessors exist: `content.as_message() -> Option<&Message>`, `content.is_message()`, `content.as_sticker()`, `content.as_poll()`, `content.is_redacted()`, `content.as_msglike()`.\n\n## 6. Send a text message\n\nTwo equivalent paths. `RoomMessageEventContent` is `matrix_sdk::ruma::events::room::message::RoomMessageEventContent`.\n\n```rust\n// A) Directly on the Room (matrix_sdk::Room). `send` takes `impl MessageLikeEventContent`,\n//    returns SendMessageLikeEvent which is IntoFuture:\nroom.send(RoomMessageEventContent::text_plain(\"hello world\")).await?;\n\n// B) Through the Timeline (adds a local echo). `send` takes AnyMessageLikeEventContent -> `.into()`:\ntimeline\n    .send(AnyMessageLikeEventContent::RoomMessage(\n        RoomMessageEventContent::text_plain(\"hello world\"),\n    )) // or: RoomMessageEventContent::text_plain(\"hi\").into()\n    .await?; // -> Result<SendHandle, Error>\n```\nContent constructors: `RoomMessageEventContent::text_plain(body)`, `::text_html(plain, html)`, `::text_markdown(md)`, `::notice_plain(body)`, `::emote_plain(body)`, `::new(MessageType)`.\n\n## 7. Media / avatars\n\n`client.media() -> Media`; `Media::get_media_content` (`matrix-sdk-0.14.0/src/media.rs`).\n\n```rust\nlet mxc: OwnedMxcUri = /* e.g. room.avatar_url().unwrap() */;\n\n// Full file:\nlet bytes: Vec<u8> = client.media().get_media_content(\n    &MediaRequestParameters {                       // ⚠️ renamed: it's MediaRequestParameters, NOT MediaRequest\n        source: MediaSource::Plain(mxc.clone()),    // ruma::events::room::MediaSource\n        format: MediaFormat::File,\n    },\n    true,                                           // use_cache: bool\n).await?;\n\n// Thumbnail (server-side resize):\nlet thumb: Vec<u8> = client.media().get_media_content(\n    &MediaRequestParameters {\n        source: MediaSource::Plain(mxc),\n        format: MediaFormat::Thumbnail(MediaThumbnailSettings::new(96u32.into(), 96u32.into())),\n        //  or: MediaThumbnailSettings::with_method(Method::Crop, w.into(), h.into())\n    },\n    true,\n).await?;\n```\n`MediaThumbnailSettings { method: Method, width: UInt, height: UInt, animated: bool }` — `::new(w,h)` uses `Method::Scale`, non-animated; `::with_method(method, w, h)` for `Method::Crop`.\n\nConvenience helpers (avoid building `MediaRequestParameters` by hand):\n```rust\nlet room_avatar: Option<Vec<u8>> = room.avatar(MediaFormat::File).await?; // Room::avatar(MediaFormat)\n\n// Member avatar:\nif let Some(member) = room.get_member(user_id).await? {   // -> Option<RoomMember>\n    let member_mxc: Option<&MxcUri> = member.avatar_url();\n    // member.display_name() -> Option<&str>, member.name() -> &str\n}\n```\n\n## 8. Sessions & E2E encryption\n\n- With **both** `sqlite` + `e2e-encryption` features on and a `sqlite_store(...)` configured, encryption is **automatic**: the crypto store (Olm/Megolm keys, account) persists in the same encrypted SQLite DB, incoming events decrypt transparently, and `room.send(...)` auto-encrypts in encrypted rooms. No extra calls needed to *receive/read* messages.\n- `EncryptionSettings` (default via `#[derive(Default)]`) — all off by default:\n  - `auto_enable_cross_signing: bool = false`\n  - `auto_enable_backups: bool = false`\n  - `backup_download_strategy: BackupDownloadStrategy = <default>` (does not auto-download backup keys)\n  Set them with `Client::builder().with_encryption_settings(EncryptionSettings { .. })`.\n- **First-pass verification:** you can ignore device verification. Decryption is *not* gated on verifying the sender's device, so messages still decrypt for known sessions. Undecryptable events surface as `MsgLikeKind::UnableToDecrypt` (missing keys, not a verification block). Verification/cross-signing lives under `client.encryption()` (`Encryption`) when you want it later.\n- Multi-process safety: set `.cross_process_store_locks_holder_name(\"my-app\")` and `SyncServiceBuilder::with_cross_process_lock()` if more than one process touches the store.\n\n## 9. Threading model\n\nYes — the SDK is **tokio-based**. Everything above marked `async` must run inside a Tokio runtime (`#[tokio::main]` or an explicit `Runtime`). `SyncService::start()` spawns long-lived background tasks onto that runtime; the diff streams (`RoomList`/`Timeline` `subscribe`) are `futures` `Stream`s you poll with `.next().await`. `Client`, `Room`, `Timeline`, and `Arc<RoomListService>` are all `Clone` + `Send`/`Sync`, so share them across tasks freely.\n\n---\n\n### Deltas from your original description, flagged\n1. `MediaRequest` → **`MediaRequestParameters`** in 0.14 (`{ source: MediaSource, format: MediaFormat }`); `get_media_content(&MediaRequestParameters, use_cache: bool)`.\n2. `TimelineItemContent` is **nested** — messages live at `MsgLike(MsgLikeContent{ kind: MsgLikeKind::Message(Message) })`, not as a top-level `Message` variant. Use `content.as_message()`.\n3. `MatrixAuth::restore_session(session, RoomLoadSettings)` needs the **second arg**; the one-arg form is `Client::restore_session(session)`.\n4. `RoomList` entries need a **filter + `add_one_page()`** on the `RoomListDynamicEntriesController` or the stream yields an empty list.\n5. `RoomListService` normally comes from `SyncService::room_list_service()` (returns `Arc<RoomListService>`), not direct construction.\n6. `LoginBuilder` is `IntoFuture` — `.login_username(..).initial_device_display_name(..).await` works directly (`.send().await` is equivalent).\n7. Unread info is a struct: `room.unread_notification_counts() -> UnreadNotificationsCount { notification_count, highlight_count }`, plus `num_unread_messages/notifications/mentions() -> u64`."}],"stop_reason":"end_turn","stop_sequence":null,"stop_details":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":2,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2885,"cache_read_input_tokens":99133,"output_tokens":8641,"server_tool_use":{"web_search_requests":0,"web_fetch_requests":0},"service_tier":"standard","cache_creation":{"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":2885},"inference_geo":"not_available","iterations":[{"input_tokens":2,"output_tokens":8641,"cache_read_input_tokens":99133,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2885,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":2885,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"type":"message"}],"speed":"standard"},"diagnostics":null},"requestId":"req_011CcmxiKWQexSmhLekaZcgD","attributionAgent":"general-purpose","type":"assistant","uuid":"466e8502-3140-4da3-8dbd-1d6f37589367","timestamp":"2026-07-07T03:10:31.614Z","userType":"external","entrypoint":"cli","cwd":"/opt/src/github/skiptools","sessionId":"13b5e524-5294-454b-b5bf-0c335b2fa97f","version":"2.1.193","gitBranch":"HEAD","slug":"swirling-swimming-lark"}
